      var clientNamesArray=[];
      var previousName=null;

   </script>   
	 <div>
	
		<div>
         <script>
            /*&lt;![CDATA[*/ 
            var clientFullName='ABIGAIL GARCES ';
            if(previousName!=clientFullName){
				clientNamesArray.push(clientFullName);
            }
            previousName=clientFullName;
			$(document).ready(function(){
				$('#applicationSearch').typeahead({
					source:clientNamesArray,
					items:50,
					matcher: function (item) {
					 var array=item.split(" ");
							 if (array[0].toLowerCase().indexOf(this.query.toLowerCase()) == 0) {
                    return ~array[0].toLowerCase().indexOf(this.query.toLowerCase());
                  } 
                  else if ( array[1].toLowerCase().indexOf(this.query.toLowerCase()) == 0){
                  	 return ~array[1].toLowerCase().indexOf(this.query.toLowerCase());
                  }
					}
				});
			});
            /*]]&gt;*/
         </script>
